Because it is a new urban area, there is no lively dining scene in the small streets and alleys around it. It is said that there is an Internet celebrity oyster next to it, so I ate it by myself, so I ate takeaway.
The decoration style of the hotel is good, with a lot of slates, the room is relatively quiet, and the overall service is very warm, especially the front desk reception. This price should be regarded as the top hotel in Zhanjiang. I will stay there next time. It is safe, quiet, and the scenery is very good. , in the middle of Chikan Old Street and French Style Street, it is very convenient to take a taxi.
The parking lot is very convenient. You can basically walk a few steps to the elevator to the lobby. After the butler maintains the license plate, it is easy to enter and exit. But don't drive to Chikan Old Street by yourself. Roads are being built throughout Zhanjiang.
Disadvantages: The facilities are slightly old, the handle of the bathtub is coming out, and the room service is a bit inexplicable. I got angry on the first day, and I put a tea bag in the bottled water every time, but it was not replenished the next day. I don‚Äôt know why. Have you forgotten the rules? The one-click room service call from the guest room's landline also didn't work. I had to ask the housekeeper for many things (luckily, I had a housekeeper who also gave me breakfast for the day).
